The first wave has a radius of %wave_initial_radius% units and deals %damage_per_wave% damage to all encompassed enemy units.  Compared to the previous wave, each subsequent wave has its radius increased by %wave_radius_increase_per_wave% units and its damage dealt increased by %damage_per_wave%, so Incinerate becomes larger and more damaging the longer it is channeled.  The cast range and maximum number of waves increase per level of Exort."
		"DOTA_Tooltip_Ability_invoker_retro_incinerate_Note0"              	"Incinerate's mechanics have been slightly altered for balance reasons.  Years ago, Incinerate's cast range, radius, and maximum number of waves all scaled with Exort, and each wave dealt a static 75 damage."
